#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: semua_data
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS semua_data;

CREATE TABLE `semua_data` (
  `id_semua` bigint(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `nama` varchar(30) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `id_th` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `id_status` int(5) NOT NULL,
  `id_setoran` int(30) NOT NULL,
  `id_admin` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `penyetor` varchar(30) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `keterangan` varchar(250) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `nominal` varchar(30) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `terbilang` varchar(50) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `tgl_bayar` varchar(11) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_semua`),
  KEY `id_admin` (`id_admin`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=2739 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_general_ci;
